    <h1>Web inputs page for Automation Testing Practice</h1>

    <div class="row mt-3">
      <p>Web inputs refer to the data or information provided by users through various input mechanisms on a website.

  <script>

    $(document).ready(function () {

      const inputNumber = $('#input-number');
      const inputText = $('#input-text');
      const inputPassword = $('#input-password');
      const inputDate = $('#input-date');


      const today = new Date();
      const dateString = today.toISOString().slice(0, 10);

      //inputNumber.val('1234');
      //inputText.val('Welcome to Practice Website');
      //inputPassword.val('SuperSecretPassword!');
      //inputDate.val(dateString);


      function resetInputs() {
        inputNumber.val('');
        inputText.val('');
        inputPassword.val('');
        inputDate.val('');
      }

      function resetResult() {
        $("#result").html("")
      }

      // first load
      resetInputs();
      resetResult();
      // or with default values
      //displayResult();

      function displayResult() {
        const outputTemplate = (outputNumber, outputText, outputPassword, outputDate) => {
          return `
      
        <div class="row mb-2">
          <div class="col">
            <label for="output-number">Output: Number</label>
            <strong class="output-box" id="output-number">${outputNumber}</strong>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="row mb-2">
          <div class="col">
            <label for="output-text">Output: Text</label>
            <strong class="output-box" id="output-text">${outputText}</strong>
          </div>
        </div>

         <div class="row mb-2">
          <div class="col">
            <label for="output-password">Output: Password</label>
            <strong class="output-box" id="output-password">${outputPassword}</strong>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div class="row mb-2">
          <div class="col">
            <label for="output-date">Output: Date</label>
            <strong class="output-box" id="output-date">${outputDate}</strong>
          </div>
        </div>
         `};
        // Get input values
        const number = inputNumber.val();
        const text = inputText.val();
        const password = inputPassword.val();
        const date = inputDate.val();


        const outputs = outputTemplate(number, text, password, date);

        $("#result").html(outputs)
      }

      $('#btn-display-inputs').on('click', function () {
        displayResult();
      });


      $('#btn-clear-inputs').on('click', function () {
        resetInputs();
        resetResult();
      });

      $("#input-number, #input-text, #input-password, #input-date").on(
        "input change keyup copy paste",
        function () {
          resetResult();
        }
      );

    });

  </script>
